---
name: ralph-tasker
description: Create and maintain Ralph task files (.ralph/ralph-tasks.md). Use ONLY when the user explicitly says “use ralph-tasker” or “use the Ralph skill.” Do not auto-trigger from tasks mode or incidental edits to .ralph/ralph-tasks.md.

# Ralph Tasker

## Overview
Define requirements and turn them into a `.ralph/ralph-tasks.md` task file for the Ralph CLI loop. Ask for missing information one question at a time, accept "Use reasonable defaults", and ensure epics include acceptance criteria tasks. Hard rule: never create tasks that require user action, approval, or validation. You are an Information Conservator, not a Summarizer: never drop or compress user-provided details. Hoard every specific detail, map it into tasks, and add color to fully flesh out a coherent, complete plan. If running inside a Ralph tasks loop, do not invoke this skill unless the user explicitly asked for it.

**Mandatory guardrails:** Every task file must begin with a **Guardrails (Non-Negotiable)** section that lists architecture constraints and strategic objectives. Every task file must also include an explicit **Constraint Check (Guardrails)** epic that enforces those guardrails. If constraints/strategy are unknown, the first use of this skill in a project must begin with interview questions to collect them.

## Workflow
1. Intake
- Ask the user to provide all available info about the work. Prompt for: goal, scope boundaries, users/personas, constraints, data sources, integrations, environments, non-goals, success criteria, deadlines, and testing expectations.
- **If constraints/strategic objectives are unknown:** ask interview questions first. Minimum set:
  - What are the **non-negotiable architecture constraints** (hosting, infra, cloud providers, cost limits)?
  - What are the **strategic objectives** that must not change?
  - What are the **non-goals / forbidden changes**?
  - What are the **compliance/security constraints** (no secrets in repo, privacy, approvals)?

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
@@ -205,2 +215,40 @@
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}
+
 function emitBacklogReorder(fromId: string, toId: string, order: string[]): void {

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}
+

   if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
   window.dispatchEvent(

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}
+

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);

+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

**Identifying potential reorder bug with mixed statuses**

Reorder logic uses a queue including items beyond backlog (like in_progress or blocked), but drag-and-drop allows only backlog items; this mismatch could cause incorrect reorder behavior. I'll need to verify if reorder should restrict to backlog items only.

+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);

+function applyBacklogOrder(items: WorkItem[], backlogOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  const backlogItems = items.filter((item) => item.status === 'backlog');
+  if (backlogItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const backlogById = new Map(backlogItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedBacklog: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of backlogOrder) {
+    const item = backlogById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of backlogItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedBacklog.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let backlogIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (item.status !== 'backlog') {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedBacklog[backlogIndex] ?? item;
+    backlogIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

thinking
**Evaluating queue item status handling**

Considering that only backlog items are draggable and reordered, it's safest to keep existing logic using all non-done statuses to avoid unexpected semantic changes. I’ll ensure reorder functions only apply to backlog items to preserve prior behavior and avoid inconsistencies with other statuses.
thinking
**Refactoring reorder to apply consistent queue ordering**

The current reorder logic risks mismatch because it reorders backlog items but the queue includes blocked/in_progress too. I'll update the reorder function to apply order to all queue items (non-done, excluding onDeck) to keep positions consistent with the visible queue and rename it to reflect this broader scope.

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);

+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);

+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }

+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {

   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {

+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+

+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }

+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+

+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);

+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

-function reorderBacklog(items: WorkItem[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): WorkItem[] {
+function reorderArray<T>(items: T[], fromIndex: number, toIndex: number): T[] {
   const next = [...items];
   const [moved] = next.splice(fromIndex, 1);
+  if (!moved) {
+    return next;
+  }
   next.splice(toIndex, 0, moved);
   return next;
 }
 
+function applyQueueOrder(items: WorkItem[], queueOrder: string[]): WorkItem[] {
+  if (queueOrder.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueSet = new Set(queueOrder);
+  const queueItems = items.filter((item) => queueSet.has(item.id));
+  if (queueItems.length === 0) {
+    return items.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+  }
+
+  const queueById = new Map(queueItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
+  const used = new Set<string>();
+  const orderedQueue: WorkItem[] = [];
+
+  for (const id of queueOrder) {
+    const item = queueById.get(id);
+    if (!item || used.has(id)) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    orderedQueue.push(item);
+    used.add(id);
+  }
+
+  for (const item of queueItems) {
+    if (!used.has(item.id)) {
+      orderedQueue.push(item);
+    }
+  }
+
+  let queueIndex = 0;
+  const nextItems = items.map((item) => {
+    if (!queueSet.has(item.id)) {
+      return item;
+    }
+    const replacement = orderedQueue[queueIndex] ?? item;
+    queueIndex += 1;
+    return replacement;
+  });
+
+  return nextItems.map((item, index) => ({ ...item, order: index + 1 }));
+}

+                                    fromQueueIndex,
+                                    toQueueIndex,
+                                    queueItems,
+                                  );
+
+                                  if (!decision.approved) {
+                                    setQueueOrderOverride(null);
+                                    setPendingReorder(null);
+                                    triggerRevertPulse();
+                                    if (fromItem) {
+                                      triggerDeniedHighlight(fromItem.id);
+                                    }
+                                    addMessage(
+                                      buildNarrationMessage(
+                                        sampleSessionId,
+                                        'chat_ai',
+                                        `Reorder denied: ${decision.reason} Keeping the current queue.`,
+                                        fromItem?.id,
+                                      ),
+                                    );
+                                    return;
+                                  }
+
+                                  const nextItems = applyQueueOrder(
+                                    backlogItems,
+                                    nextQueueOrder,
+                                  );
+                                  setBacklogItems(nextItems);
+                                  setQueueOrderOverride(null);
+                                  setPendingReorder(null);
+                                  emitBacklogReorder(
+                                    draggedId,
+                                    item.id,
+                                    nextQueueOrder,
+                                  );
+                                  if (fromItem && toItem) {
+                                    const direction =
+                                      fromQueueIndex < toQueueIndex ? 'after' : 'before';
+                                    addMessage(
+                                      buildNarrationMessage(
+                                        sampleSessionId,
+                                        'chat_ai',
+                                        `Reorder approved. "${fromItem.title}" now sits ${direction} "${toItem.title}".`,
+                                        fromItem.id,
+                                      ),
+                                    );
+                                  }
+                                } catch (error) {
+                                  setQueueOrderOverride(null);
+                                  setPendingReorder(null);
+                                  triggerRevertPulse();
+                                  if (fromItem) {
+                                    triggerDeniedHighlight(fromItem.id);
+                                  }
+                                  addMessage(
+                                    buildNarrationMessage(
+                                      sampleSessionId,
+                                      'chat_ai',
+                                      'Reorder denied due to a review error. Keeping the current queue.',
+                                      fromItem?.id,
+                                    ),
+                                  );
+                                }
+                              })();
                             }}
                             onDragEnd={() => {
                               setDraggedId(null);
